<li><a href="/wiki/Gianni_Morandi" title="Gianni Morandi">Gianni Morandi</a> (singer, born 1944)</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Ludovico_Morbioli" title="Ludovico Morbioli">Ludovico Morbioli</a> (Catholic layman, declared Blessed, 1433–1485)</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Edgardo_Mortara" class="mw-redirect" title="Edgardo Mortara">Edgardo Mortara</a> (Catholic priest that was the subject of the <i>Mortara Case</i> during the <a href="/wiki/Risorgimento" class="mw-redirect" title="Risorgimento">Risorgimento</a>, 1851–1940)</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Gianluca_Pagliuca" title="Gianluca Pagliuca">Gianluca Pagliuca</a> (footballer, born 1966)</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Pier_Paolo_Pasolini" title="Pier Paolo Pasolini">Pier Paolo Pasolini</a> (writer, poet, director, 1922–1975)</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Roberto_Regazzi" title="Roberto Regazzi">Roberto Regazzi</a> (luthier, born 1956)</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Guido_Reni" title="Guido Reni">Guido Reni</a> (painter, 1575–1642)</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Ottorino_Respighi" title="Ottorino Respighi">Ottorino Respighi</a> (composer, 1879–1936)</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Augusto_Righi" title="Augusto Righi">Augusto Righi</a> (physicist, authority on <a href="/wiki/Electromagnetism" title="Electromagnetism">electromagnetism</a>, 1850–1920)</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Carlo_Ruini" title="Carlo Ruini">Carlo Ruini</a> (equine anatomist, 1530–1598)</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Angelo_Schiavio" title="Angelo Schiavio">Angelo Schiavio</a> (footballer, 1905–1990, scored the winning goal in extra time in the <a href="/wiki/1934_FIFA_World_Cup_Final" title="1934 FIFA World Cup Final">1934 World Cup Final</a>, played only for <a href="/wiki/Bologna_F.C._1909" title="Bologna F.C. 1909">Bologna</a>)</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Elisabetta_Sirani" title="Elisabetta Sirani">Elisabetta Sirani</a> (painter, 1638–1665)</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Alberto_Tomba" title="Alberto Tomba">Alberto Tomba</a> (skier, born 1966)</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Ondina_Valla" title="Ondina Valla">Ondina Valla</a> (first Italian woman Olympic gold medalist, 1916–2006)</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Mariele_Ventre" title="Mariele Ventre">Mariele Ventre</a> (teacher and educator, founder of <a href="/wiki/Piccolo_Coro_dell%27_Antoniano" class="mw-redirect" title="Piccolo Coro dell' Antoniano">Piccolo Coro dell' Antoniano</a> choir, 1939–1995)</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Christian_Vieri" title="Christian Vieri">Christian Vieri</a> (footballer, born 1973)</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Vitale_da_Bologna" title="Vitale da Bologna">Vitale da Bologna</a> (painter, fl. 1330, d. 1361)</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Anteo_Zamboni" title="Anteo Zamboni">Anteo Zamboni</a> (anarchist who at the age of 15 attempted to assassinate Benito Mussolini, 1911–1926)</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Alex_Zanardi" title="Alex Zanardi">Alex Zanardi</a> (racing driver, born 1966)</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Marco_Aurelio_Zani_de_Ferranti" title="Marco Aurelio Zani de Ferranti">Marco Aurelio Zani de Ferranti</a> (writer, musician, and composer, 1801–1878)</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Alessandro_Carloni" title="Alessandro Carloni">Alessandro Carloni</a> (director, animator, artist who worked on films like <i><a href="/wiki/Kung_Fu_Panda" title="Kung Fu Panda">Kung Fu Panda</a></i> and <i><a href="/wiki/The_Croods" title="The Croods">The Croods</a>,</i> born 1978)</li>
</ul>
<p>In addition to the natives of the city listed above, the following have made Bologna their home:</p>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Giosu%C3%A8_Carducci" title="Giosuè Carducci">Giosuè Carducci</a> (poet and academic, Nobel Prize for Literature, born near Lucca, Tuscany, 1835–1907)</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Carlo_Felice_Cillario" title="Carlo Felice Cillario">Carlo Felice Cillario</a> (Italian conductor of international renown, founder of the Bologna Chamber Orchestra in 1946 (7 February 1915 – 13 December 2007)</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Umberto_Eco" title="Umberto Eco">Umberto Eco</a> (writer and academic, born in Alessandria, Piedmont, 1932–2016)</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Enzio_of_Sardinia" class="mw-redirect" title="Enzio of Sardinia">Enzio of Sardinia</a> (born c. 1218, King of <a href="/wiki/Kingdom_of_Sardinia" title="Kingdom of Sardinia">Sardinia</a> and illegitimate son of Emperor Frederick II, was imprisoned in <a href="/wiki/Palazzo_Re_Enzo" title="Palazzo Re Enzo">Palazzo Re Enzo</a> from 1249 until his death in 1272)</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Vasco_Errani" title="Vasco Errani">Vasco Errani</a> (politician, born 1955)</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/William_Girometti" title="William Girometti">William Girometti</a> (painter, born in Milan, 1924-1998)</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Alfonso_Lombardi" title="Alfonso Lombardi">Alfonso Lombardi</a> (sculptor, born in Ferrara, c. 1497–1537)</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Niccol%C3%B2_dell%27Arca" title="Niccolò dell'Arca">Niccolò dell'Arca</a> (sculptor, born in Bari, c. 1435/1440–2 March 1494)</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Juan_Ignacio_Molina" title="Juan Ignacio Molina">Juan Ignacio Molina</a> (naturalist, born in <a href="/wiki/Chile" title="Chile">Chile</a>, 1740–1829)</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Giovanni_Pascoli" title="Giovanni Pascoli">Giovanni Pascoli</a> (poet and academic, born in San Mauro di Romagna, 1855–1912)</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/St._Petronius" class="mw-redirect" title="St. Petronius">St. Petronius</a> (San Petronio, bishop of <a href="/w/index.php?title=Bishopric_of_Bologna&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Bishopric of Bologna (page does not exist)">Bologna</a> and patron saint of the city, birthplace unknown, died c. 450 AD)</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Romano_Prodi" title="Romano Prodi">Romano Prodi</a> (economist, politician, born in Scandiano, Reggio Emilia, 1939)</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Gioachino_Rossini" title="Gioachino Rossini">Gioachino Rossini</a> (opera composer, born in Pesaro, 1792–1868)</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Giuseppe_Torelli" title="Giuseppe Torelli">Giuseppe Torelli</a> (composer, born in Verona, 1658–1709)</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Wu_Ming" title="Wu Ming">Wu Ming</a> (collective of writers, active since 2000)</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Farinelli" title="Farinelli">Farinelli</a> (Carlo Broschi, castrato opera singer, 1705–1782)</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Cesare_Cremonini_(musician)" title="Cesare Cremonini (musician)">Cesare Cremonini</a> (songwriter, 1980)</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Lucio_Dalla" title="Lucio Dalla">Lucio Dalla</a> (singer-songwriter, musician and actor, 1943-2012)</li>
</ul>
